    <div class="post-content">
      <p><em><strong>Work in Progress</strong></em></p>
<p>I am just trying to understand the gnostic mythology here.
Some of this rings true for me. Other bits I am asserting as mere theory.</p>
<p>Since delving into the Nag Hammadi Library I
have simultaneously been encouraged and
&lsquo;challenged&rsquo;. But I am understanding.</p>
<p>Before the Gospel of Philip (further down the page), I will make some disclaimers.</p>
<p>Firstly, this document appears to be a dialogue, so it&rsquo;s reasonable to also
reason about it, rather than take it as hard-fact.</p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">2
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">3
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">4
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">5
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">6

<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>I find fault with the others who say that it
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>will not rise.
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Then both of them are at fault.
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>You say that the flesh will not rise.
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But tell me what will rise, that we may honor
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>you.</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>

<h2 id="sysygies-and-pleromas">Sysygies and pleromas</h2>
<h3 id="new-testament">New Testament</h3>
<p>Jesus embodies the full Pleroma; Represents God the Father.</p>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pleroma">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pleroma</a></p>
<dl>
<dt>Colossians 1:19</dt>
<dd>19 For in him all the fullness of God was pleased to dwell,</dd>
<dt>Colossians 2:9</dt>
<dd>9 For in him the whole fullness of deity dwells bodily,</dd>
<dt>Ephesians 4:13</dt>
<dd>13 until all of us come to the unity of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God, to maturity, to the measure of the full stature of Christ.</dd>
<dt>Colossians 2:10</dt>
<dd>10 and you have come to fullness in him, who is the head of every ruler and authority.</dd>
</dl>
<p>etc.</p>
<h3 id="valentinianism">Valentinianism</h3>
<p>Each individual has his or her Pleroma or spiritual counterpart.</p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">

<h2 id="the-virgin-birth">The Virgin Birth</h2>
<dl>
<dt><a href="https://biblehub.com/matthew/1-18.htm">Matthew 1:18-25</a></dt>
<dd>20: But just when he had resolved to do this, an angel of the Lord appeared to him in a dream and said, &ldquo;Joseph, son of David, do not be afraid to take Mary as your wife, for the child conceived in her is from the Holy Spirit.</dd>
</dl>
<p>I believe Jesus was conceived by the Holy
Spirit; The Holy Spirit providing the miracle
of lack of human father.</p>
<p>I also believe that his virgin birth and resurrection may be
mirrored/imitated through Him prototypically, while we live
and breathe in this life; This constituting the Way.</p>
<p>In this <a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Brief%5FSummary%5FTheology.htm">summary of Valentinians theology</a> here, it somewhat explains this.</p>
<h3 id="the-holy-spirit-catalyst-for-transformation">The Holy Spirit; Catalyst for transformation</h3>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">2
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">3
</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Holy Spirit shepherds everyone and rules         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>all the powers, the &#34;tame&#34; ones and the &#34;wild&#34;       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ones, as well as those which are unique.             |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>This is how I think it works.</p>
<p>The Gospel of Matthew is explicit in that
Jesus was conceived of the Holy Spirit.</p>
<p>The Gospel of Philip suggests that the Holy
Spirit is female, and contests that Jesus could not have been
conceived of the Holy Spirit.</p>
<p>But I think The Holy Spirit is more likely to
be a male/female syzygy, as are other holy
spirits; For example, heavenly angels are also &lsquo;holy&rsquo;
spirits.</p>
<p>The Holy Spirit is another emanation of God, as is Jesus, and according to Valentinianism, Sophia.</p>
<p>When the Holy Spirit descended on Mary and
Jesus&rsquo; physical body was was conceived without a human father; It was a miracle.</p>
<p>Like sudoku, the blank was filled by the miracle, and Jesus was born.</p>

<li><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Brief%5FSummary%5FTheology.htm">http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Brief%5FSummary%5FTheology.htm</a></li>

</ul>
<p>Jesus was conceived in the physical realm as a result of the
catalyst of the Holy Spirit filling in the
blank (This is just my theory).</p>
<p>No reason yet to believe Jesus had a
distinctly separate divine parent other than
God the Father (who&rsquo;s title Father, I believe
is represents parenthood, not gender).</p>
<p>In this I tally 3 Holy personages of God:</p>
<ul>
<li>God the Father</li>
<li>God the Son</li>
<li>Holy Spirit</li>
</ul>
<p>And the lesser emanation, Sophia:</p>
<ul>
<li>Sophia (made of Spirit) (but <a href="https://www.bibliotecapleyades.net/mistic/pistis%5Fsophia/ps073.htm">redeemed already, purportedly</a>; According to <a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/pistis-sophia/">Pistis Sophia</a>)
<ul>
<li><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Valentinian%5FSacramental.htm">Valentinians believed</a> Sophia&rsquo;s descent resulted in creation of material substance, repentance gave rise to soul and Sophia&rsquo;s gnosis gave rise to spirit.</li>
<li><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Demiurge.htm">The Demiurge in Valentinianism - Valentinus and the Valentinian Tradition</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>So that still makes for a Holy Trinity, actually, in my opinion.</p>
<ul>
<li>The Demiurge
<ul>
<li>According to Valentinianism is not a direct emanation from God
<ul>
<li>Emanated from Sophia in her fallen state; So is created hylic</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/ptolemy-to-flora/">Ptolemy to Flora // Bodacious Blog</a></li>
<li><a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/the-tripartite-tractate/">The Tripartite Tractate // Bodacious Blog</a></li>
<li><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Demiurge.htm">The Demiurge in Valentinianism - Valentinus and the Valentinian Tradition</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>I am personally not <strong>strongly</strong> attached to doctrine of <strong>only</strong> 3 personages of
God (i.e. the Trinity), but I haven&rsquo;t had
strong evidence to suggest more than that
either.</p>
<p>Sophia seems plausible to me, but I wouldn&rsquo;t
bundle in with the Trinity.</p>
<p>As for the Demiurge; I have no evidence for
the demiurge at all, but neither strong
evidence that it wouldn&rsquo;t exist.</p>
<h3 id="the-bridal-chamber">The Bridal Chamber</h3>
<p>Similarly to Jesus&rsquo; conception, the Holy Spirit acts
through the Bridal Chamber to fill in our blank.</p>
<p>I think of the Holy Spirit as the aspect of God that is there during the wedding ceremonies.</p>
<p>I believe this results in a double-marriage;
Firstly to divine self, and then to God the
Son due to <em>compatibility of syzygy to syzygy</em>
(my own theory).</p>
<p><em>All redeemed spirits are syzygies</em> (my own
theory), but the human spirit is fallen, and
is not initially a syzygy (perfect/complete). The divine self (a
person&rsquo;s &lsquo;angel&rsquo;) is also fallen and not a
syzygy. When reunited into a syzygy, they
become one and can return to God, the highest
aeon who is also a syzygy. In heaven there is
no male or female because they&rsquo;re undivided.</p>
<p>I believe the Holy Spirit descends, and
amends a person, and then may indwell in them.</p>
<p>We received a repaired spiritual body, or
received a spiritual body in entirety, and the
Holy Spirit may also repair physical physical
ailments and keep our bodies healthy.
Jesus received a physical body on descent; He
was always Spirit, and unlike us started out in this
world already perfect/complete.</p>
<p>A person becomes spiritually reunified, a syzygy.
With Jesus&rsquo; birth, the miracle was more of a generative one. He received a physical father and physical body.</p>
<p>The virgin birth is contested mystery.
The Gospel of Philip says Jesus could not have been conceived of the Holy Spirit because they believe the Holy Spirit is explicitly female.
But I think the Holy Spirit is more likely to be a syzygy, like God, but a catalyst for transformation, an agent of change, and a Witness.
The Holy Spirit descends on a person and fills in the blank - which is a miracle.</p>
<p>For me it descended and filled in the blank which is my spiritual other female half
and then in the Bridal Chamber, united me with God as well.</p>
<p>I can say im not a heretic because I can both believe
that the Holy Spirit conceived Jesus and the
Gospel of Philip is correct for the most part too.</p>
<p>The Holy Spirit then is able to work through us as an agent of change
because It becomes compatible to dwell in a person.</p>
<p>A male/female syzygy is compatible with the
male/female syzygy that is the Holy Spirit,
and also Jesus who is a syzygy; And we are one in Christ Jesus.</p>

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>When we were Hebrews, we were orphans and had
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>only our mother, but when we became
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Christians, we had both father and mother.</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>In this theory, Sophia, twin divine Aeon of
Jesus, is our spiritual Mother, and to reverse
the fall (damage done from procreation outside
of the Bridal Chamber), we may be spiritually bonded to
Jesus through the Bridal Chamber, and when we
die, adopted by the Father, and we are all
reconciled syzygies; Christ is the Father,
though, and adoption happens when you&rsquo;re
saved - you spiritually die in this life and are born again.</p>
<p>According the Gospel of Philip, humans are
born with a spiritual mother (Sophia), but without a
spiritual Father, but God adopts and fixes us.</p>
<p>The miracle of the missing component is provided by the Holy Spirit, through belief in Jesus.</p>
<p>According to my theory,
in the fall, sin has either effectively spliced the human spirit in
half, or left humans with a spirit of only one half of a complete syzygy, disconnecting from the Father (because
God the Father is Truth and completeness, and sin is error),
and sin still latches on to people until
their spiritual redemption, preventing them
from being redeemed (reunited), until they
receive grace.</p>
<p>I consider Sophia to be mere hypothetical mythology.
However, I&rsquo;m convinced the Bridal Chamber is a thing.</p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">

<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>Thus Eve separated from Adam because it was          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>not in the bridal chamber that she united with       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him.                                                 |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>Disconnection since the fall.</p>
<p>Thus the alchemical marriage that takes place in Holy Spirit baptism is a double marriage between:</p>
<ul>
<li>You (Bridegroom) + Divine self (Bride/Angel)</li>
<li>(You + Divine self; Syzygy) + (God the Son; Syzygy)</li>
</ul>
<p>And physical reality, modelled after spiritual reflects this.</p>
<p><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Valentinian%5FSacramental.htm">Valentinian Sacramental Practice</a></p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1

<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>a person could enter the Fullness and be
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>permanently joined with the bridegroom angel
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>while still in the flesh</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>And I&rsquo;m guessing the words bride/bridegroom are interchangeable and don&rsquo;t reflect physical appearance.</p>
<p>With the Holy Spirit acting as the arbitrator/divine matchmaker/Advocate/Witness.</p>
<p>Fallen people and their spiritual counterpart are not spiritually unified.</p>
<p>Lastly, when a redeemed person dies, there is another spiritual marriage to God the Father:</p>
<ul>
<li>Body of Christ: (You + Divine self) + (God the Son) + (Sophia, according to Valentinian Christianity)
<ul>
<li>Bride</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>God the Father
<ul>
<li>Bridegroom</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>So the Holy Spirit is able to fix a person with whatever missing piece it is that they lack, through faith in Jesus.
But they must be ready to receive it (i.e. they must repent of sin, so the piece can be received); Water baptism first (repentance), followed by holy spirit baptism (redemption).</p>

<p><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Sophia%5FEve.htm">Sophia</a> is also redeemed.</p>

</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>Accordingly, &#34;when Sophia (Wisdom) receives
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>her consort and Jesus receives the Christ and
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the seeds and the angels; then the Fullness
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>will receive Sophia (Wisdom) joyfully, and the
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>All will come to be in unity and
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>reconciliation&#34; (Valentinian Exposition 39)</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<h3 id="sophia--twin-divine-aeon-of-jesus">Sophia (twin divine Aeon of Jesus?)</h3>
<p>Best to read this before taking my notes on it:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Sophia%5FEve.htm">http://gnosis.org/library/valentinus/Sophia%5FEve.htm</a></li>
</ul>
<!--listend-->
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 2
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 3
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 4
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 5
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 6
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 7
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 8
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f"> 9
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">10
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">11
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">12
</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Gospel of Philip states that &#34;Eve
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>separated from Adam because she was never
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>united with him in the Bridal Chamber&#34;(Gospel
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of Philip 70). According to Valentinian myth
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the fall, God held back perfect knowledge
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(gnosis) of himself from his Aeons (including
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Sophia) so that they would search for him.
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Until Chist manifested himself to them, the
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Aeons had not united in the &#34;bridal chamber&#34;,
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a metaphor for perfect knowledge of God. It
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was as a result of this withholding of gnosis
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that the fall occured.</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>The Apocryphon of John</dt>
<dd>According to The Apocryphon of John, one of the main texts of Gnosticism dating to circa 180, Sophia represented divine wisdom and the female spirit.</dd>
</dl>
<p>Present in creation.</p>
<dl>
<dt><a href="https://www.biblegateway.com/passage/?search=Proverbs%208&amp;version=NIV">Proverbs 8</a></dt>
<dd>I was there when he set the heavens in place, when he marked out the horizon on the face of the deep, 28 when he established the clouds above and fixed securely the fountains of the deep, 29 when he gave the sea its boundary so the waters would not overstep his command, and when he marked out the foundations of the earth.</dd>
</dl>
<p>I&rsquo;m not sure if this proverb strongly implies
the existence of Sophia.</p>
<p>We are not supposed to pray to Sophia either, but to God the Father.</p>

<p>I personally do not find not a lot of sense in this.</p>
<h2 id="glossary">Glossary</h2>
<p>Types and images are mentioned fairly
frequently in Gospel of Philip.</p>
<p>This is what I have managed to divulge.</p>
<h3 id="types">Types</h3>
<p><a href="https://www.bibliotecapleyades.net/mistic/pistis%5Fsophia/ps135.htm">Pisis Sophia</a></p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">

</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">2

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>me, lest one of our kinsmen should be in such
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a type, and have mercy with all the souls
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which shall be in this type;</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<h3 id="the-image">The image</h3>
<ul>
<li>&ldquo;image and the angel are united with one another&rdquo;</li>
<li>&ldquo;unite the angels with us also, as being the images.&rdquo;</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="on-reincarnation">On reincarnation</h2>
<p>Since the Gospel of Philip may imply reincarnation.</p>
<h3 id="hebrews-10">Hebrews 10</h3>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1
</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>Just as man is appointed to die once, and after that to face judgment,</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>The Apostle Paul seems to imply there is no such thing.</p>
<h3 id="pistis-sophia">Pistis Sophia</h3>
<p><a href="https://www.bibliotecapleyades.net/mistic/pistis%5Fsophia/ps140.htm">https://www.bibliotecapleyades.net/mistic/pistis%5Fsophia/ps140.htm</a></p>
<p>Pistis Sophia, on the other hand, talks about
it; But not as something which often occurs.</p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">2
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">3
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">4
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">5
</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>I have turned Elias and sent him into the body
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of John the Baptizer, and the rest also I
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>turned into righteous bodies, which will find
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the mysteries of the Light, go on high
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and inherit the Light-kingdom.</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>I&rsquo;m personally inclined to believe that
reincarnation of a sort, <strong>may</strong> occur but, even if it does,
not perpetually, and not without consequences,
<a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/astral-projection-pt-2/">due to this</a> experience I had.</p>
<p>Pistis Sophia suggests that before the world
is dissolved, a person may be reincarnated,
but that a person should not tie day-to-day,
or cycle-to-cycle, due to the risk of not having
anther opportunity.</p>

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>If her husband loves her, then they resemble         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>her husband.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>If it is an adulterer, then they resemble the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>adulterer.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Frequently, if a woman sleeps with her husband       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>adulterer with whim she usually has                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>intercourse, the child she will bear is born         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>resembling the adulterer.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being.                                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>light.                                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He who begets, begets in private, and he             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself is hidden, since [...] image.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But one who begets, begets children in               |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>another man, but even if she slips out of her        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>foreskin, teaching us that it is proper to           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>destroy the flesh.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Most things in the world, as long as their           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>inner parts are hidden, stand upright and            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>live.                                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>If they are revealed, they die, as is                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>illustrated by the visible man: as long as the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>intestines of the man are hidden, the man is         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>alive; when his intestines are exposed and           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>come out of him, the man will die.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>So also with the tree: while its root is             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hidden, it sprouts and grows.                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>If its root is exposed, the tree dries up.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>So it is with every birth that is in the             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>world, not only with the revealed but with the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hidden.                                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For so long as the root of wickedness is             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hidden, it is strong.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But when it is recognized, it is dissolved.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>When it is revealed, it perishes.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>That is why the Word says, &#34;Already the axe is       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>laid at the root of the trees&#34; (Mt 3:10).            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>again - but the ax penetrates deeply, until it       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brings up the root.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Jesus pulled out the root of the whole place,        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>while others did it only partially.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the root.                                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It will be plucked out if we recognize it.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But if we are ignorant of it, it takes root in       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>us and produces its fruit in our heart.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It masters us.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>We are its slaves.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It takes us captive, to make us do what we do        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>not want; and what we do want, we do not do.         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is powerful because we have not recognized        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it.                                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>While it exists it is active.                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Ignorance is the mother of all evil.                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Ignorance will result in death, because those        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who come from ignorance neither were nor are         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>nor shall be.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>[...] will be perfect when all the truth is          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revealed.                                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For truth is like ignorance: while it is             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hidden, it rests in itself, but when it is           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revealed and is recognized, it is praised,           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>inasmuch as it is stronger than ignorance and        |

<h2 id="i-believe-i-have-received-the-light-if-the-gospel-of-philip-is-accurate">I believe I have received the light, if the Gospel of Philip is accurate</h2>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">2
</span></code></pre></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>If anyone becomes a son of the bridal chamber,       | https://mullikine.github.io/posts/astral-projection/
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he will receive the light.                           |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<p>I believe that the &rsquo;light&rsquo; the Gospel of
Philip talks about is the lighted up vesture
of the soul, which is certainly able to be
activated, especially by remembrance of the
experience; The body floods with electricity.</p>
<p>This is the &lsquo;feeling&rsquo; of it I would say.
But I do not care so much for that - only the mission - to <a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/astral-projection-pt-3/">become love</a>;
To become a teacher and a healer.
To not forget who Jesus is.</p>
<h2 id="notable-passages">Notable passages:</h2>
<dl>
<dt><a href="http://gnosis.org/library/actphil.htm">Acts of Philip</a></dt>
<dd>For the Lord said to me: Unless ye make that which is beneath to be above, and the left to be right (and the right left), ye shall not enter into my kingdom. Be like me in this: for all the world is turned the wrong way, and every soul that is in it.</dd>
</dl>
<p>Eat/know the word of Jesus, and accept the Holy Spirit to receive life:</p>
<dl>
<dt><a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/gospel-of-philip/">Gospel of Philip</a></dt>
<dd>&ldquo;Flesh and blood shall not inherit the kingdom of God&rdquo; (1 Co 15:50). What is this which will not inherit? This which is on us. But what is this, too, which will inherit? It is that which belongs to Jesus and his blood. Because of this he said &ldquo;He who shall not eat my flesh and drink my blood has not life in him&rdquo; (Jn 6:53). What is it? His flesh is the word, and his blood is the Holy Spirit.</dd>
</dl>
<p>Philip makes an explicit claim that Jesus&rsquo; blood is the Holy Spirit.
That <strong>may</strong> be the case.
Jesus is one with God the Father.
God the Father is Spirit.
Jesus&rsquo; blood is spirit, I believe that too.
It&rsquo;s all connected somehow.</p>
<p>However, is it going to far to have conceptualise this too explicitly?</p>
<ul>
<li>Lay hands to gift the Holy Spirit</li>
<li><a href="https://www.blueletterbible.org/Comm/stewart%5Fdon/faq/introduction-to-the-gifts-of-the-holy-spirit/13-do-people-receive-the-holy-spirit-or-spiritual-gifts-by-the-laying-on-of-hands.cfm">Do People Receive Either the Holy Spirit, or Spiritual Gifts, by the Laying on of Hands? by Don Stewart</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="links">Links</h2>
<p>I agree with the following exegesis / eisegesis.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.gnosticdoctrine.com/2019/12/truth-and-nakedness-gospel-of-philip.html">Gnostic Doctrine Gnostic Christianity: Truth and Nakedness The Gospel of Philip</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Put on the light:</p>
<dl>
<dt><a href="http://gnosis.org/naghamm/gop.html">Gospel of Philip</a></dt>
<dd>Some are afraid lest they rise naked. Because of this they wish to rise in the flesh, and they do not know that it is those who wear the flesh who are naked. It is those who [&hellip;] to unclothe themselves who are not naked.</dd>
</dl>
<p>Salvation is the garment.</p>
<p>The blood of Jesus is the garment.
-   Ask to be washed in it</p>
<p><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Rr7Udj8lEUU">Peter in Jail - YouTube</a></p>
<p><a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/astral-projection-pt-2/">Astral Projection Part 2 - Sacred Kiss, Healing, Resurrection // Bodacious Blog</a></p>
<hr>
<dl>
<dt>Water, fire and light</dt>
<dd><figure><img src="https://mullikine.github.io/ox-hugo/water-fire-light.png"/>
</figure>
</dd>
</dl>
<p>See: <a href="https://mullikine.github.io/posts/kingdom-of-god/">https://mullikine.github.io/posts/kingdom-of-god/</a></p>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">

<p>What is on us is this fleshly garment that we wear.</p>
<h3 id="we-can-still-touch-jesus-astral-garment-just-saying">We can still touch Jesus&rsquo; <code>astral</code> garment; Just saying :)</h3>
